msg:Because I arrived late, I checked in after 2 o'clock in the morning. At the front desk, I saw a few tenants saying that the air conditioner was not cool and needed to change rooms.
Then I thought to myself that I should not be given a room with a broken air conditioner,
After entering the room, I turned on the air conditioner, and found that there was a sound from the air outlet. At that time, the temperature in the room was displayed at 28 degrees. I thought it should be fine, so I washed and fell asleep.
As a result, I was woken up by the heat at 6 o'clock in the morning! Get up and take a look, the indoor temperature is 29 degrees! That said the air conditioner was totally useless! The sound is not cooling! Such a big hotel, the air conditioner is broken in summer, I was shocked, can this be considered a 5-star hotel?
At 6:00 in the morning, I was tired and sleepy, and I didn't have the energy to change the room. I closed my eyes and slept for a while, and it was still 28 degrees after 8:00. I was really speechless. When I checked out, I told the front desk that the air conditioner was broken, and told me to change the room when I checked in next time. Then why did I open a room to the user when I knew the air conditioner was broken? Didn't sleep well after spending money!
I will never stay again in my life!
Other facilities inside have been around for a long time. For example, the water in the sink is also broken, and it can only leak little by little. The carpet is yellow and black. name:Aâ€nâ€oâ€nâ€yâ€mâ€oâ€uâ€sâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Executive Suite
info:Stayed in May 2022
info:Other
info:35 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted May 13, 2022
msg:Shanxi Wanshi Jinghua Hotel, as a Taiyuan native, I don't care every time I pass by, and I don't know it is a five-star hotel. I am fortunate to stay and share my experience this time. First of all, the parking lot is right in front of the hotel, and the parking space is very wide. Walking into the lobby, I feel some sense of age in it, but I still prefer to stay in such a five-star hotel with a sense of age. The front desk is a bit stingy, it is too close to the door, and check-in is very fast. This time, the room 1707 on the 17th floor is a suite. The first impression when I get out of the elevator is that the ceiling is really low. I can reach the top with my hand at 170 degrees. When entering the room, although the ceiling is not too high, it is stronger than the corridor. The entrance is a living room, and the bedroom is inside. Although the area is small, the space layout is very reasonable, and there is no crowding. The overall facilities are relatively old, and the bathtub in the bathroom is lower and smaller. Fortunately, I don't like to take a bath at ordinary times, and friends who like to take a bath should be careful. This is the first time I have stayed in a hotel with a laptop in the room. At first, I thought it was the wrong room, but later I found out that it was a laptop provided by the hotel. In terms of bedding, the bed is moderately firm, the pillows are good, and the quilt is a little thin. In terms of breakfast, I booked a room without breakfast, so I didn't eat it, so I won't make a comment here. In general, if you like nostalgia, you can try it. If you are looking for a five-star experience, it is not recommended. Besides, the price is also put here, and the new five-star at this price will not come down. All in all, a very good stay experience!
